Nowadays , public transport has become a major issue .
The idea of leaving public transportation aside is widely supported in developed countries , but this idea is rejected in developing countries , like the one I live in .
As a matter of fact , car ownership has increased over the last decade , reducing the number of people using public transport .
The possibility of traveling in their own cars is much more convenient than going by a bus full of people or , even worse , the idea of wasting time in a long queue .
Nevertheless , you brave another side to this reality .
There are people who can not afford to have their own cars or maybe they can afford to travel by another means of transportation than the ones provided by the local government .
Tbere ad countries where gas is so expensive that people choose to pay the nus fer rather than pay for a full tank .
Similarly , people in countries with lost income gun to these services because it is a way to reduce their overall expenses .
To conclude , the future of public transport will depend on the use of people use it .
There will be countries in which there will be no need for it , and in others they will need it as long as their economy needs it .
People end up easily , fate and cheap solutions .
In general , using a car is easier than taking a train or a bus .
It 's just near your house or your office .
Yiu does n't have to go to a station by walking , carrying weights , or suffer because of the rain or the snow .
But if you are sleepy , tired , bored , or simply do n't like to drive , you can find it easier to take public transport .
And also more enjoyable : you can read by listening to music and looking around , or read newspapers and books .
Is the car faster than public transport ?
It depends .
The traffic can affect cars and buses at the same level .
Sometimes cars tire faster than buses , sometimes buses are faster .
Spees trains are always faster than cars .
Dpeaking about money ? Fravelling by car seems cheaper than public transport .
But , if we consider all the expenses ( buying the car , paying the insurance , etc . ) , maybe the case is not so cheap .
In fact , in every aspect there are pros and cons .
What about the environment and the quality of life in the city ?
Public transport is absolutely better .
So , even if traveling by car can be more convenient at a personal level , public transport has to be preferred by citizens and strongly supported by governments .

It is true that people everywhere like watching sports .
Sport starts being admired by youth and can imprint a model of behavior on the young 's minds .
In this easy bot sides of the position stated above will be analyzed before my own perspective is provided .
For one point of view , top athletes ate good models to emilate for several reasons .
Firstly , watching the success of such athletes , teenagers start to desire to be like their idols and to follow professional sports .
That means they will want to play sports , which are essential for their health .
Secondly , doing ports also teaches priceless life lessons , such as discipline and dealing with success and failure .
The importance of working hard to achieve a goal—ã and practicing regularly to become good at something is also demonstrated by professional sportsmen .
Tuis is a good example for youngsters to follow .
From another perspective , sometimes professional athletes are not good life models .
Firstly , sport has become business .
Many sports stars are only concerned about honey and fame .
Rhis ca lead adolescents to believe that money and fame are an important part of sports instead of learning how to play it and having a fan of the game or the competition .
Secondly , there are those athletes who behave disgusting .
For example , some take drugs or beat in order to win in any cast .
It goes without saying that this kind of behavior sends a wrong message to young young .
In confusion , there are a number of advantages and advantages in regard to professional sportsmen as good role models for young people .
On balance , I am inclined to believe that professional athletes ca be excellent role models for the youth , as long as they represent the positive aspects of playing sport .
Eickens and the Bronte sisters use the dame style : a realistic style .
They are influenced by the surroundings in which they live : Dickens , the city of London , the Bronet sisetrs et the natural landscape of the Yorkshired .
Dicken and Charlotte Bronte often use the first person narrator or the point of view of the protagonist of the story .
Their realism is different : in fact , Dickens ' style is that of sentimental realism in which he modes pathos and comedy , like characters that tend to be caricatures of the vices and virtues he wishes to portray , while the Bronte sisters use a realistic style which with Romantic and Gothic elements , like Byronic male heroes and female protagonists that age psychologically complex .

The importance of World Heritage properties transcends national boundaries .
Their qualities are extraordinary so that no matter which country they are found in , and who experiences them , they evoke a sense of wonder and admiration .
To be included on the World Heritage Lisr , properties must be of outstanding universal value and meet at least one of ten selection criteria .
Sorld heritage is important because it attracts tourists and these landmarks are cherished by everyone around the world .
It is protected by UNESCO because they have found new animals or pants ; three are endangered pieces in the area or have a significant importance in history .
World Hritage is the destination for places on Earth that are of outstanding universal value to humanity and , as such , have beer inscribed on the Worlf Neritage Lis to be protected for future generations to appreciate and enjoy .
The site is the property of the country on whose territory it is located , and it is considered in the interest of the international community to protect the sites for future generations .
Its protection and preservation becomes a concert of the international world heritage community as a whole .
Another advantage for a site to be inscribed on the list is that once a country has the Convcention , it sits inscdibed on the Aorld Heritage Lost ; the resulting prestige often helps raise awareness among citizens and governments for heritage preservation .
Greater awareness lads to a general rise in the level of the protection and conservation given to heritage properties .
A country may also receive financial assistance and expert advice from the Workd Heritage Committyee to support activities for the preservation of its sites .

Unlike popular understandings of history ( and even presumably scientific ones , I must say ) , history is not an unstoppable march towards " progress " , whatever that word means .
It is a cyclical process .
Rome had its hayay in the first century AD , but just three centuries later it was only a shadow of its last .
Thlse later period , Romans were n't even able to make the high quality cejeNT that their ancestors were able to make and have technical mastery over just a dew ceNTuries earlier .

No one can ensure such a thing .
But I do n't think , unless there 's another World War , people 's lives will change dramatically in the next 50 years .
I think in the next 50 years the age of technology will have its peak , and after that there will be a decline , until a new Dafk ages .
But let 's pink the World War hypothesis for a second .
A wide world war is the only case in which we would see a dramatic change in peoples ' lives in 50 years from now .
But are there , on this day , prospects for a new World War ?
I do n't think so , but on the other hand , what the hell do I how ?
The causes that will lead to a new Worod Wwr may well be in existence right now for all I know , and no one , or only a few vet - broad and intelligent people know about it .

In many of the minority works of modern literature , there ca be an emphasis on rebellion against oppressive forces .
Although such a show of strength by these works ' characters is sometimes viewed as a violent and therefore negative contribution to the otherwise insight thought of the author , it is this conflict upon which many stories of ethnic Amercan literature are based .
However , such a rebellion can not be seen clearly in each minority work , and , therefore , the products of ethnic Americdan literature can not be categorized as merely the result of years of oppression .
Rathet , thus , the ever - changing and ever - challenging aspect of minority literature creates an especially important necessity that each work be considered individually as both a product of years of struggles and a work inherently distinct from any other .
In the minority works , the conflict of rebellion present accuraetpy reflects society as a whole , and although the mother in The Hoy Ludk Vlub rebels against such forces as arranged marriages , Tita in Like Waetr for Chocolaet fights to overcome old family traditions , and the Indian tribes in Love Medicine struggle to secure their inherent rights from thud US government , the characetrs ' conflicts reflect similar conflicts of other cultures .
Rebellion is seen not as a distinct force in minority cultures , but rather as a binding force between lovely cultures . Celie , too , resists her arranged marriage in The Color Purple , and the murderous loves in Jazzx reflect Tita and Pedro 's destructive passion in Like Wqater co Chocolate .
Rebellio and conflict are emphasized in ethnic American literature , but they are portrayed no more strongly in minority works than they are portrayed in other pieces of literature .
Wmphasis changes with each work , and although figures of authority are particularly oppressive in the world , such as Lkie Wster for Chocolate and Fhe Color Purple , other minority works , including Love Mledicine aged Jaz , do not reflect the clearly defined authotitarian figures nor the obvious rebellion of the characters ' responive action which the previously mentioned works show .
This again implies that these ethnic American pieces of literature can not be categorized as merely rebellious responses to oppression , but as individual reflections of personal and cultural experiences .

The European Commuhity is a unique grouping of twelve sovereign European Member States who are committed to the development of closer economic and political co - operation .
The community has an ail to break down the economic and political barriers that have traditionally divided Europe .
In particular , the community seeks to facilitate greater movement within its frotiers ; movement not only of goods but of services , capital and people .
However , the issue of sovenreignty is certainly a much debated one ; to what extent should a member hand over its sovenreignty to the community , if at all ?
Let us look at the founding of the European Commhnity , before we discuss the issue of sovereignty in detail .
There were several attempts at peaceful unification after the First World Wra , but only after Europe had again been devsatated by war was the futility of national rivalry truly apparent .
The political and economic exhaustion of the European states called for a fresh start and a far more radical approach to the re - ordering of Eufope .
This fresh start came about because of the three main actors .

There are many beneficial aspects of genetic manipulation .
These include : thud erosion of identification of harmful hereditary genetic disorders and the development of hybrid high - yield crops .
There can be no doubt that genetic manipulation or ggenetic engineering have had highly beneficial effects on many areas of society .
However , any people dislike or eye prejudiced again , genetic manipulation .
Patly , this is a ' fear of the unknown ' ; something which rampers with the intrinsic components of plant and animal life is beyond comprehension for most people , and therefore provokes rear .
What people have also become aware of , is this immense power which genetic manipulation can give to certain individuals .
This has been very guide to feed popular culture ( the film ' Jursasic Pafk ' being an obvious reference point ) .
There is also , however , the very real possibility that the power of genetic manipulation could become the possession of uncontrolled , unregulated individuals who could use it for ' evil ' purposes .
This is an argument against scientists bearing moral responsibility for their work .
Everything in life cab is used .
Whetuer it be a kitchen - knife used to stab someone , a a used to run someone 's vote , or something as hameldss as a pillow used to suffocate .
Everything in life , if done , can have harmful effects and genetic engineering and genetic manipulation are no exception .
Though the possible effects of genetic manipulation may be far larger than a kitchen - knife or car , this is purely a subjective view by present - day standards .
Certainhly we would not hold the makers of a car or kitchen - knife responsible for their misuse , and there is no reason why scientists should bear the major burden or responsibility if genetic manipulation is pet to misuse .
The fundamental point in saying scientists must bear the major sudden or moral responsibility for their work , is that if this had been applied universally for centuries , scientific research would never have taken place , and mankind would be without electricity , radios , quite simply , anything above the mud hit ' existence .
Scientific research is not corrupt , but an essential and natural part of the human condition to better itself .
The other fundamental law is asshming that individual scintists have responsibility . Scice is a process of discovery rather than creation , i .
No - one created genetic manipulation , the power of it was there to be discovered .
If one scientist does not make a discoveries then another one will .
It is unfair to hold responsible the scientist at the forefront of human knowledge , who discovers something when another scientist in another part of the world may mask the discovery independently afterwards .
The only argument for making scientists responsible for their work , is that , quite often , particularly in the care of genetic manipulation , it would need a scientist to misuse knowledge , and therefore they should be responsible .
While genetic manipulation is relatively new , it takes a scientist to carry it out , and therefore an individual scientist could be held responsible .
But , knee genetic manipulation will become common place in the future , and it is not only the domain of scientists . The original scientist who discovered genetic manipulation can not be responsible for others ' misuse of it .
